FIX messages and feeds them into Camel routes.\n */\npublic class FixConsumer extends DefaultConsumer {\n\n    private static final Logger LOG = LoggerFactory.getLogger(FixConsumer.class);\n\n    public FixConsumer(FixEndpoint endpoint, Processor processor) {\n        super(endpoint, processor);\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    public FixEndpoint getEndpoint() {\n        return (FixEndpoint) super.getEndpoint();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStart() throws Exception {\n        LOG.info(\"Starting FIX consumer for session: {}\", getEndpoint().getSessionID());\n        super.doStart();\n    }\n\n    @Override\n    protected void doStop() throws Exception {\n        LOG.info(\"Stopping FIX consumer for session: {}\", getEndpoint().getSessionID());\n        super.doStop();\n    }\n\n    /**\n     * Processes an inbound FIX message by creating an Exchange and routing it through Camel.\n     *\n     * @param  message   the FIX message received\n     * @param  sessionID the FIX session ID\n     * @throws Exception if processing fails\n     */\n    public void onMessage(Message message, SessionID sessionID) throws Exception {\n        if (!isStarted()) {\n            LOG.warn(\"Received FIX message but consumer is not started, ignoring: {}\", message);\n            return;\n        }\n\n        LOG.debug(\"Received FIX message: {} from session: {}\", message, sessionID);\n\n        Exchange exchange = getEndpoint().createExchange();\n        exchange.getIn().setBody(message);\n        exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SESSION_ID, sessionID != null ? sessionID.toString() : null);\n        if (sessionID != null) {\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_SENDER_COMP_ID, sessionID.getSenderCompID());\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_TARGET_COMP_ID, sessionID.getTargetCompID());\n        }\n\n        try {\n            String msgType = message.getHeader().getString(quickfix.field.MsgType.FIELD);\n            exchange.getIn().setHeader(FixConstants.FIX_MESSAGE_TYPE, msgType);\n        } catch (Exception e) {\n            LOG.debug(\"Could not extract MsgType from FIX message\", e);\n        }\n\n        try {\n            getProcessor().process(exchange);\n            if (exchange.getException() != null) {\n                getExceptionHandler().handleException(\"Error processing FIX message\", exchange, exchange.getException());\n            }\n        } finally {\n            releaseExchange(exchange, false);\n        }\n `fixVersion` (default \"FIX.4.2\"), `heartBeatInterval` (default 30), `socketConnectHost`, `socketConnectPort`.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixComponent.java (new)\n```java\n@Component(\"fix\")\npublic class FixComponent extends DefaultComponent {\n    @Override\n    protected Endpoint createEndpoint(String uri, String remaining, Map<String, Object> parameters) throws Exception {\n        FixConfiguration configuration = new FixConfiguration();\n        setProperties(configuration, parameters);\n        FixEndpoint endpoint = new FixEndpoint(uri, this, configuration);\n        endpoint.setSessionID(remaining);\n        setProperties(endpoint, parameters);\n        return endpoint;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixEndpoint.java (new)\n```java\n@UriEndpoint(firstVersion = \"4.18.0\", scheme = \"fix\", title = \"FIX\",\n             syntax = \"fix:sessionID\", category = { Category.MESSAGING })\npublic class FixEndpoint extends DefaultEndpoint {\n    @UriPath @Metadata(required = true) private String sessionID;\n    @UriParam private FixConfiguration configuration;\n    // createProducer() -> new FixProducer(this)\n    // createConsumer() -> new FixConsumer(this, processor)\n}\n```\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixConsumer.java (new)\nExtends `DefaultConsumer`. Receives inbound FIX messages via `onMessage(Message, SessionID)`, creates Camel Exchange with message body and header constants, and routes through processor.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/java/org/apache/camel/component/fix/FixProducer.java (new)\nExtends `DefaultAsyncProducer`. Implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)`. Extracts `quickfix.Message` from exchange body, resolves `SessionID` from configuration or headers, looks up the FIX `Session`, and sends the message.\n\n### components/camel-fix/src/main/resources/META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix (new)\n```\nclass=org.apache.camel.component.fix.FixComponent\n```\n\n## Analysis\n\n### Implementation Strategy\n\nThe `camel-fix` component is implemented as a new, clean FIX protocol component for Apache Camel that follows the exact same conventions as the existing `camel-quickfix` component but with a simplified, more direct API.\n\n**Architecture decisions:**\n\n1. **Extends `DefaultComponent`**: The `FixComponent` extends `DefaultComponent` as required, uses the `@Component(\"fix\")` annotation for service discovery via Camel's SPI mechanism. The component creates `FixEndpoint` instances by parsing the URI's `remaining` part as the session ID.\n\n2. **Extends `DefaultEndpoint`**: The `FixEndpoint` uses `@UriEndpoint` with `scheme = \"fix\"` and `syntax = \"fix:sessionID\"`. It stores a `FixConfiguration` instance for endpoint-level parameters. The URI path parameter is the session ID.\n\n3. **Extends `DefaultConsumer`**: The `FixConsumer` provides `onMessage(Message, SessionID)` as the entry point for inbound FIX messages. It creates Camel `Exchange` objects populated with the FIX message body and relevant headers (`CamelFixMessageType`, `CamelFixSessionID`, `CamelFixSenderCompID`, `CamelFixTargetCompID`).\n\n4. **Extends `DefaultAsyncProducer`**: The `FixProducer` implements `process(Exchange, AsyncCallback)` as required by the task. It extracts `quickfix.Message` from the exchange body and resolves the target `SessionID` either from the endpoint configuration or from message headers. It uses `Session.lookupSession()` from QuickFIX/J to find the active session.\n\n5. **`FixConfiguration` with `@UriParams`**: The configuration POJO groups all URI parameters. Fields include `configFile`, `senderCompID`, `targetCompID`, `fixVersion` (default \"FIX.4.2\"), `heartBeatInterval` (default 30 seconds), `socketConnectHost`, and `socketConnectPort`.\n\n6. **`FixConstants` as header constants**: String constants following Camel's `CamelXxx` naming convention for all FIX-related message headers.\n\n### Integration with Parent Build\n\n- `components/pom.xml` updated to include `<module>camel-fix</module>` in alphabetical order between `camel-file-watch` and `camel-flatpack`\n- `camel-fix/pom.xml` inherits from the `components` parent POM and declares QuickFIX/J dependencies using the `${quickfixj-version}` property defined in the parent\n- The service descriptor file at `META-INF/services/org/apache/camel/component/fix` enables Camel's service loader to discover the component by scheme name \"fix\"\n\n### Dependencies\n\nThe component depends on:\n- `camel-support`: Provides `DefaultComponent`, `DefaultEndpoint`, `DefaultConsumer`, `DefaultAsyncProducer` base classes\n- `quickfixj-core`: QuickFIX/J core library for FIX protocol support (`Session`, `SessionID`, `Message`)\n- `quickfixj-messages-all`: All FIX message type definitions\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":107,"cache_read_input_tokens":108181,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":107,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":24,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"fa040a28-50ee-45c8-91ad-af77a24cd6d1","uuid":"19362f3d-136c-432d-99f6-46f146f4fdf6"}
